There is also an amusement park, an aquarium, and an indoor ski resort, so it is great for families to travel and enjoy.
The hotel is located next to a small lake, so you can take a light walk, and the hotel's swimming pool and gym are clean and nice to use. Moreover, the pool water is not cold, making it even better for enjoying with children. There is also a small but playroom for children next to the gym.
The room has a veranda, and as it faces the lake, you can see the sunrise and sunset, making it great for relaxation.
Lastly, the breakfast room is a space that is neither too big nor too small, so it was nice to enjoy a variety of food, but there was only one coffee machine, so there was a waiting line, and the coffee quantity was set to small, which was disappointing.
